    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 42pt 0pt 0cm">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       主要内容
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">

    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      第一部分
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      网络安全综述（第
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      1
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      章）
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      第二部分
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密码学基础（第
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      2
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      章
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ~
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      第
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      4
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      章）
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      第三部分
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      网络安全应用（第
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      章
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ~
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      第
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      7
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      章）
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      第四部分
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      系统安全机制（第
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      8
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      章
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ~
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      第
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      11
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      章）
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      第五部分
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      代码安全（第
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      12
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      章
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ~
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      第
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      14
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      章）
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      第六部分
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      其它安全主题（第
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      16
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      章
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ~
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      第
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      17
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      章）
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>

      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       《网络安全与保密》
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
        <font face="Times New Roman">
        </font>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       胡建伟
      </span>
      <font face="Times New Roman">
      </font>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       编
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
        <font face="Times New Roman">
        </font>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       西安电子科技大学出版社
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       讲授内容：
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">

    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 18pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文隶书; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      理论部分：
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       第一周
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt">
      </span>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要点
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       网络安全的基本概念
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       网络安全的目标
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        3
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       网络安全与协议层次的关系
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要求
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       掌握网络安全的目标及措施
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       能够举出网络安全的实例并简要说明
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        3
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       掌握不同协议层次上的网络安全问题
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       讲授内容
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US">
      1.1
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      基本概念
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US">
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      例子
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      保护私人住所
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      挂窗帘
      <span style="mso-tab-count: 1">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      防止外人偷窥
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      加锁
      <span style="mso-tab-count: 1">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      防小偷
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      养狼狗
      <span style="mso-tab-count: 1">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      拒绝不受欢迎之客
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      安装警报系统，摄像头
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      检测不速之客
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      电围墙，篱笆，门卫
      <span style="mso-tab-count: 1">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      审查
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      安全应考虑的问题的两方面（矛盾与统一）：安全威胁、被保护物品的价值
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      安全措施的目标：Access Control，Authentication，Integrity，Accountability，Privacy
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      职业前景：网络安全管理；网络安全软件设计开发；网络律师；网上监管专家
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 157.5pt; TEXT-INDENT: -136.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -13.0; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      与网络安全有关的著名公司：Symantec(赛门铁克)、Microsoft、Kaspersky、Redhat、McAfee Versign……
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      国外著名公司漏洞统计数据；漏洞实例分析
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      区分：远程管理（控制）软件vs黑客软件，木马
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      常见网络安全用语，俗语说明：木马（trojan），特洛伊、肉鸡
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      隐私、言论自由、版权
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      1.2 网络拓扑与安全
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      什么是拓扑
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      网络按照基本拓扑的分类：星型、总线型、环型
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      其他：网状，不规则型
     </span>
    </h2>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">
       拓扑与网络安全的关系
      </span>
      <span style="mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      星型网的优势：所有两个节点间通信只定义了一条路径
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 105pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 10.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      网络（特指中间节点）处于固定的物理位置，易确保物理安全
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      TCP/IP 协议进行通信；因特网上的安全隐患
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      按照TCP/IP的协议层次，安全隐患问题分以下来讨论
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 52.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 5.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      网际层、传输层、应用层、
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 52.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 5.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US">
      CERT/CC
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US">
      ：
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Computer Emergency Response Team/Coordination Center
      </span>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 52.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 5.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US">
      http://www.cert.org
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      1,网际层:
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      伪造（假冒）IP地址
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      伪造（假冒）ARP
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      伪造（假冒）路径控制信息
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 6.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      恶意使用（假冒）源路由
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 6.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      利用IP/ICMP数据包的DoS攻击（非授权使用）
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      2，传输层:
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      预测（假冒）TCP初始序号
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 6.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      利用TCP/UDP数据包的DoS攻击（非授权使用）
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      3，应用层:
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      扫描/搜索（非授权使用）
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 6.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      DNS（Domain Name Service:域名服务）欺骗（假冒）
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 6.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      窃听用户认证信息（窃听）
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 6.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      攻击程序缺陷（非授权使用）
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 6.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      代理服务器的非法使用（非授权使用）
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 6.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      利用电子邮件进行的DoS攻击（非授权使用）
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 6.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      病毒与木马
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      1.3 网络安全的层次结构(Hierarchy of Network Security)
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      物理安全
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      安全控制
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      安全服务
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      1.4 网络安全威胁
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      1.4.1
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      网络威胁的类型
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      窃听、假冒、重放、流量分析、破坏完整性
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      1.4.2
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      威胁的动机(Motives)
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      工业间谍、财政利益、报复或引人注意、恶作剧、无知
     </span>
    </h2>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span style="mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">
      <font face="Times New Roman" size="3">
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       第二周
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt">
      </span>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要点
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       网络攻击及其分类
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       客户服务器的工作模式及其特点
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要求
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       掌握主动攻击与被动攻击的区别并能举例说明
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       能够针对客户和服务器进行区分并能编程
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       讲授内容
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      1.5 网络攻击
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      “攻击”的定义
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      任何非授权行为
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      法律定义：入侵行为完全完成且入侵者已经在目标网络内部。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      本课程：可能使一个网络受到破坏的所有行为都被认为是攻击。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      网络攻击的两大分类
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      被动攻击(Passive Attacks)：攻击者监视所有信息流以获得某些秘密
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      形式：窃听、流量分析
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      最难被检测到
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      主动攻击(Active Attacks)：攻击者试图突破你的安全防线
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      形式：假冒、重放、欺骗、消息篡改、拒绝服务等
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      对网络的被动攻击和主动攻击
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      1.7 基本安全技术
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      防火墙(Firewall)，加密(Encryption)，身份认证(Authentication)，数字签名(Digital Signature)，内容检查(Content Inspection)
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      1.5 网络攻击
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      “攻击”的定义：任何非授权行为
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      法律定义：入侵行为完全完成且入侵者已经在目标网络内部。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      本课程：可能使一个网络受到破坏的所有行为都被认为是攻击。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      有关对网络的被动攻击和主动攻击的词汇：
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US">
      Normal Flow
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US">
      ；
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Interception
      </span>
      ；
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Interruption
      </span>
      ；
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
       </span>
       Modification
      </span>
      ；
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Fabrication
      </span>
      ；
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US">
      Model for Network Security
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US">
      ；
      <span lang="EN-US">
       Network Access Security Model
      </span>
      ；
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      ***应用层的客户-服务器方式
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      在 TCP/IP 的应用层协议使用的是：客户-服务器方式
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      计算机的进程(process)就是运行着的计算机程序。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      为解决具体应用问题而彼此通信的进程称为“应用进程” 。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      应用层的具体内容就是规定应用进程在通信时所遵循的协议。
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      客户和服务器的区分
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      客户(client)和服务器(server)都是指通信中所涉及的两个应用进程。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      客户-服务器方式所描述的是进程之间服务和被服务的关系。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      客户是服务请求方，服务器是服务提供方。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      客户软件的特点：在进行通信时临时成为客户，但它也可在本地进行其他的计算。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      被用户调用并在用户计算机上运行，在打算通信时主动向远地服务器发起通信。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      可与多个服务器进行通信。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      不需要特殊的硬件和很复杂的操作系统。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 42pt; TEXT-INDENT: -21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -2.0; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      服务器软件的特点 ：专门用来提供某种服务的程序，可同时处理多个远地或本地客户的请求。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      在共享计算机上运行。当系统启动时即自动调用并一直不断地运行着。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      被动等待并接受来自多个客户的通信请求。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      一般需要强大的硬件和高级的操作系统支持。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      客户进程和服务器进程使用 TCP/IP 协议进行通信
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      功能较强的计算机可同时运行多个服务器进程
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      1.6 网络安全模型
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      考虑信息系统的四方模型:
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      Sender（发信者）、Receiver（收信者）、Enemy（敌人）、Boss（监控管理方）
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      1.8 安全漏洞
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      信息系统的安全漏洞主要有三个方面 ：
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      1）OS
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      操作系统
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      2）Network
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      计算机网络
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      3）DBMS
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      数据库管理系统
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      补充内容：
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      星号（*）密码的破解；一个电影网站的破解录像；网络嗅探器sniffer；Java编程初步
     </span>
    </h2>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt">
      <strong>
       <font face="Times New Roman">
       </font>
      </strong>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       第三周
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt">
      </span>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要点
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       对称密码系统的特点和代表算法
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       古典密码的例子：凯撒密码
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        3
        <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
        </span>
        DES
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       算法描述
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要求
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       区分对称密码系统和非对称密码系统
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       针对古典密码编程实现
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        3
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       了解
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        DES
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       算法的特点及使用方法
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       讲授内容
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      2.1
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      前
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      言
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      传统的密钥加密解密系统都是对称密钥密码系统。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      加密和解密使用同一把密钥
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      从最早的凯撒密码到使用最多的
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      DES
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，以及下一代密码算法
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Rijndael
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      1976
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      年，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Diffie
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      和
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Hellman
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      发表论文
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      “New Direction in Cryptography”,
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      从而出现了非对称密钥密码系统
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密钥加密系统的几个部分：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      M(Message)
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      消息空间，
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       C(Cipertext)
       <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密文空间
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      K(Key)
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密钥空间
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      E(Encryption Algorithm)
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      加密算法
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      D(Decryption Alorithm)
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      解密算法
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      它们满足
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      EK1(M)=C
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      DK2(C)=M
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      DK2(EK1(M))=M
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      两种密钥算法体制
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      对称密钥算法：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      K1
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       ß
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      K2
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      也叫秘密密钥算法，单一密钥算法
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      非对称密钥算法
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      K1
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       ß
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      /
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Wingdings; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
      <span style="mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Wingdings">
       à
      </span>
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      K2
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      也叫公开密钥算法
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      2.1.2
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      古典密码
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      替换密码
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      例：凯撒密码
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      置换密码
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      例：纵行置换密码
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      凯撒密码
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ----
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      简介
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      凯撒密码
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      是罗马扩张时期由
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Julius Caesar
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      创造的，用于加密通过信使传递的作战指令。
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      它把字母表中的字母移动一定位置而实现加密。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h6 align="left" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: auto; LINE-HEIGHT: normal; TEXT-ALIGN: left; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd; mso-pagination: none; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-para-margin-top: 0cm; mso-para-margin-right: 0cm; mso-para-margin-bottom: .0001pt">
     <span style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      如向右移动
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       2
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      位，则
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       A
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      变成
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       C
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       B
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      变成
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       D … X
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      变成
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       Z
       <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
       </span>
       Y
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      变成
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       <span lang="EN-US">
        Z
       </span>
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      变成？
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
     </span>
    </h6>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      凯撒密码
     </span>
