     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ----
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      分析
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      字母表总共有
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      26
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      个字母
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      用凯撒密码加密，如果明文字符串是“
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Hello
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ”
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ,
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      移动
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      2
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      位则变为密文
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      如何解密？只要将字母向相反方向移动同样位数即可
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      这里移动的位数“
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      2
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ”是加密和解密共用的密钥
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      凯撒密码
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ---
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      编程思路
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Step1:
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      读取要加密的字符串、密钥
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Step2:
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      取出字符串中的每个字符
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Step3:
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      对每个字符进行移位
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      这里采用
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Java
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      编程实例说明：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Step1 Step2 Step3
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      编译并运行程序
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      加密：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Java Caesar
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      明文
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密钥
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      解密：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Java Caesar
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      明文
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      -
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密钥
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      这里明文指“要加密的字符串”；密钥指“移动的位数”
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ***DES
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      （数据加密标准）：最通用的对称密码体制算法：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      DES--Data Encryption Standard
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密钥长度为
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      56
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      位，分组长度
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      64
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      位，需要进行
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      16
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      轮加密迭代的对称密钥加密分组算法。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      对称密码算法的两种类型：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      分组密码：一次处理一块输入，每个输入块声称一个输出块，典型例子：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      DES
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      算法
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      流密码：对输入元素连续处理，同时产生连续单个输出元素。典型例子：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      A5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      算法
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      2.2.4
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      DES
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的工作模式
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ECB (Electronic Codebook)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      电子密码本
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      CBC (Cipher Block Chaining)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密码分组链接
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      CFB (Cipher Feed back)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密文反馈
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      OFB (Output Feed back)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      输出反馈
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      有关
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      DES
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的破解
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      早期官方的得出了十分乐观的结论；
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Diffie
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Hellman
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      等修改了他们的估计；计算机科学家
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Tanenbaum
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      指出，即使没有这种专用机，也可以用穷举法破译
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      DES
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      。
     </span>
     <span style="mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt">
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -13.45pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.28">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      2.3
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      A
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      算法
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      序列密码简介
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: -13.45pt; mso-char-indent-count: -1.28">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      2.4
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      其它对称密码算法
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      2.4.1
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      IDEA
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 23.95pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; mso-para-margin-left: 2.28gd">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IDEA
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      即国际数据加密算法，它的原型是
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      PES
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，对
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      PES
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      改进后的新算法称为
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPES
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，并于
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      1992
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      年改名为
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IDEA(International Data Encryption Algorithm)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      补充内容
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Word
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密码的破解；网络嗅探器
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      sniffer
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ；
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Java
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      编程初步
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt">
      <strong>
       <font face="Times New Roman">
       </font>
      </strong>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       第四周
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt">
      </span>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要点
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       单向散列函数原理与应用
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       单向散列函数安全性分析
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要求
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       理解和掌握单向散列函数的原理和常用算法
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       了解密码破解的原理和防范与应用
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       讲授内容
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <font size="3">
       单向散列函数的原理和应用场合
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      单向散列函数：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      散列值是由单向散列函数产生的。所谓的单向散列函数
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (Hash Function
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，又称哈希函数、杂凑函数
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      )
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，是将任意长度的消息
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      M
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      映射成一个固定长度散列值
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      h
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的函数：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      h=H(M)
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      其中，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      h
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的长度为
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      m
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      单向散列函数算法
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      MD5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      和
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      SHA-1
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的算法描述
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      MD5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的前景
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      在
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      2004
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      国际密码学会议（
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Crypto’2004
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ）上， 
  
    王小云 
  教授公布了破解
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      MD5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      算法的研究成果，引起了密码学界轰动。但这里
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      MD5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      算法的破解对实际应用的冲击要远远小于它的理论意义，不会造成
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      PKI
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      、数字签名安全体系的崩溃。
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      MD5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的安全性问题
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      MD5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的两种常用的应用场合为：单向变换用户口令；对信息进行签名
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      单向散列函数的强度体现在它能把任意的输入随机化到什么程度，并且能产生输出。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      对
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      MD5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的普通直接攻击（野蛮攻击）穷举可能的明文产生和
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      H(m)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      相同的结果
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      对
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      MD5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的生日攻击：用概率来指导散列冲突的发现
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      其它对
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      MD5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的攻击：微分攻击被证明对
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      MD5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的一次循环有效，但对全部
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      4
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      次循环无效。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      有一种成功的
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      MD5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      攻击，不过是它对
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      MD5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      代码本身作了手脚，属于
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      crack
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      而不是
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      hack
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h4 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      口令长度和信息论：根据传统信息论，英语每个
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      8-bit
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      字母的信息熵为
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      1.3bits
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      （来源于英语语法的规律性这个事实，字母出现的概率不等造成了熵的减小，如果
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      26
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      个字母出现的概率均等，信息熵会增至
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      4.7bits
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ）。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密码系统的选择与密码攻击
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      对于一个密码系统来说，如果新的密码系统的强度依赖于攻击者不知道算法的内部机理，那这密码注定会失败。最好的算法是那些已经公开的，并经过世界上最好的密码分析家们多年的攻击，但还是不能破解的算法。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密码攻击
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密码分析攻击分类（都假设密码分析者知道所用的加密算法的全部知识）
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      唯密文攻击
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (cipher text only)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      已知明文攻击
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (known plain text)
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      选择明文攻击
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (chosen plain text)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      选择密文攻击
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (chosen cipher text)
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      自适应选择明文
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      /
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      密文攻击
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (chosen text)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      选择密钥攻击
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (chosen key)
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      软磨硬泡攻击
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (Rubber-hose)
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      补充内容
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      黑客字典介绍；
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Java
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      编程初步；远程控制举例；
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      VMWare
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      介绍
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      虚拟机软件介绍：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      VMWare
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      虚拟机软件可以在一台电脑上模拟出来若干台
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      PC
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，每台
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      PC
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      可以运行单独的操作系统而互不干扰，实现一台电脑
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      “
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      同时
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ”
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      运行几个操作系统，还可以将这几个操作系统连成网络。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      VMWare
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的使用：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Guest OS
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，模拟的硬件，可以使用
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ISO
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      文件作为光盘，运行模式
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      网络设置方式：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Bridged
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      方式，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      NAT
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      方式
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>

    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">

    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要点
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
