    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       公钥密码体制的原理和代表算法
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        RSA
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       和
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
       Diffie-Hellman
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
        <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
       Diffie-Hellman
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
       算法的安全性分析
       <span lang="EN-US">
       </span>
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
       3
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
       数字签名介绍
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要求
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       理解和掌握
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        RSA
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       算法和
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
       Diffie-Hellman
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       理解防范
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
       Diffie-Hellman攻击的方法
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
      <font size="3">
       3 了解数字签名的分类与应用
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       讲授内容
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      公钥密码体制的历史和发展，参考文献
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      公钥密码系统原理：基于陷门单向函数的概念。单向函数是易于计算但求逆困难的函数，
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      公钥密码系统的应用：通信保密、数字签名、密钥交换
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      密钥交换
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      通信双方交换会话密钥，以加密通信双方后续连接所传输的信息。一般，每次逻辑连接使用一把新的会话密钥，用完就丢弃。例如：Diffie-Hellman密钥交换
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      公开密钥算法RSA的描述
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      选择两个不同的大素数p和q(一般都为100位左右的十进制数字)，计算乘积：n=pq
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      和欧拉函数值：φ (n)=(p−1)(q−1)
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      随机取一整数e，1＜e＜φ (n)，且e和φ (n)互素。此时可求得d以满足：
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      ed==1 modφ(n)
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      则 d = e–1 modφ(n)
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      这样可以把e和n作为公开密钥，d作为私人密钥。其中，p、q、φ(n)和d就是秘密的陷门(四项并不是相互独立的)，这些信息不可以泄露。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      RSA加密消息m时(这里假设m是以十进制表示的)，首先将消息分成大小合适的数据分组，然后对分组分别进行加密。每个分组的大小应该比n小。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      设ci为明文分组m加密后的密文，则加密公式为
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      ci=mie (mod n)
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      解密时，对每一个密文分组进行如下运算：
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      mi=cid (mod n)
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      加/解密方案的可行性证明可以参考参考资料。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      RSA应用举例：选p=5，q=11，则
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      n=pq=55，φ (n)=(p−1)(q−1)=40
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      于是明文空间为在闭区间[1, 54]内且不能被5和11整除的数。选择e=7，则d=23。由加/解密公式可以得到加密表如表4-1所示。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      4.2
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      Diffie-Hellman密钥交换
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      算法概述
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      Diffie-Hellman算法的安全性在于在有限域上计算离散对数非常困难。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      (1)Alice和Bob协商一个大素数p及p的本原根a，a和p可以公开；
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      (2)Alice秘密产生一个随机数x，计算X=ax mod p，然后把X发送给Bob；
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      (3)Bob秘密产生一个随机数y，计算Y= ay mod p，然后把Y发送给Alice；
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      (4)Alice计算k=Yx mod p；
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      (5)Bob计算k'=Xy mod p。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      k和k'是恒等的，因为k= Yx mod p=(ay)x mod p=(ax)y mod p= Xy mod p= k'
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      则k和k'即为秘密密钥。
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      4.2.2
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      针对Diffie-Hellman算法的中间人攻击
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      4.2.3
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      认证的Diffie-Hellman密钥交换---针对中间人攻击
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US">
      4.2.4
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US">
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      三方或多方
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US">
      Diffie-Hellman
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      4.3 数字签名
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      数字签名的基本概念
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      数字签名与传统签名的比较
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      数字签名的分类
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      数字签名的方式：直接数字签名；仲裁数字签名
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      安全性： 无条件安全的数字签名； 计算上安全的数字签名
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      可签名次数：一次性的数字签名； 多次性的数字签名
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      数字签名算法：普通数字签名算法EIGamal RSA DSS/DSA
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      其他：不可否认的数字签名算法；群签名算法；盲签名算法
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      补充内容：Java实现的RSA加密和解密；Java实现的Diffie Hellman密钥分配
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
     </span>
    </h2>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <strong>
      第六周
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       ~
      </font>
      第九周
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要点
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
        <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
        </span>
        TCP/IP
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       相关网络体系结构及协议复习
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
        <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
       漏洞扫描与端口扫描
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
       3
       <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
       各种协议漏洞及其防范方法介绍
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要求
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       理解和掌握
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        TCP/IP
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       网络基础知识中有关网络安全的内容
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       理解和掌握端口扫描的作用和应用
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
      <font size="3">
       3 了解协议的漏洞分析方法，掌握防范方法及工具应用
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       讲授内容
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TCP/IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      协议栈
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      通常被认为是一个四层协议系统。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      UDP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      和
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TCP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的对比
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 16pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: .24gd">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      UDP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ：面向无连接，传送数据前不需先建立连接，不可靠，只提供
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      “
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      尽最大努力服务
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ”
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h4 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 11.25pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0; mso-para-margin-left: 1.07gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      但实现简单，速度快，开销小
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h4 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TCP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ：面向连接，传送数据前建立连接，传送结束后释放连接，复杂性和开销都比
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      UDP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      大
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h4 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      但能提供可靠的全双工信道
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      有关运输层：
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      端口的概念
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      端口就是运输层服务访问点
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TSAP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      端口是用来标志应用层的进程。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 31.5pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 3.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      端口号：端口使用
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      16bit
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的端口号进行标志。端口号只具有本地意义，即端口号只是为了标志本计算机应用层中的各进程。在因特网中不同计算机的相同端口号是没有联系的。分为两类：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      一类是所谓的熟知端口
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       ,
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      数值为
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      0~1023—&gt;
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      常用熟知端口
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (well-known port)
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      其他的端口都属于一般端口，用来随时分配给请求通信的客户进程。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      互联网地址
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      地址是在全世界范围是惟一的
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      32 bit
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的标识符。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 31.5pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 3.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      每一类地址都由两个固定长度的字段组成，其中一个字段是网络号
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      net-id
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，而另一个字段则是主机号
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      host-id
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，它标志该主机（或路由器）。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      常用的三种类别的
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      地址的使用范围
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      协议封装
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TCP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      传给
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的数据单元称作
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TCP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      报文段或简称为
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TCP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      段
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (TCP Segment)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      传给网络接口层的数据单元称作
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      分组
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (IP Datagram)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h4 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 2.0gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      更准确地说，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      和网络接口层之间传送的数据单元应该是包
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (Packet)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      。包既可以是一个
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      数据报，也可以是
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      数据报的一个片
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (Fragment)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      通过以太网传输的比特流称作帧
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (Frame)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h4 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      以太网数据帧的物理特性是其长度必须在
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      46
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ～
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      1500
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      字节之间
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      协议
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 1.0; mso-para-margin-left: 1.28gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      网际协议
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      是
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TCP/IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的核心，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      协议是不可靠的协议。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 1.0; mso-para-margin-left: 1.28gd">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      数据包中含有发送它的主机的
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      地址
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      源地址
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      )
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      和接收它的主机的
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      地址
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      目的地址
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      )
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      TCP协议
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      TCP数据包中包含序列号和应答号；排序；重传。
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      用三次握手建立 TCP 连接
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      TCP 连接释放的过程
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      TCP 的正常的连接建立和关闭
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      TCP的有限状态机模型
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      补充：IP和地理位置的对应关系；IP数据库；VisualRoute等软件介绍
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      漏洞扫描相关知识与端口扫描软件PortScanner,SuperScan简介
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      扫描（scan）就是对计算机系统或者其他网络设备进行安全相关的检测，以找出安全隐患和可被黑客利用的漏洞。扫描软件是一把双刃剑．
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      扫描的种类
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      分为三类：
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      第一类 数据库安全扫描器；
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      第二类 操作系统安全扫描器；
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      第三类 网络安全扫描器（针对子网络服务、应用程序、网络设备和网络协议等）。
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      端口扫描（Port Scan)
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      常用的端口扫描技术:
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      TCP connect()扫描；TCP SYN扫描；TCP FIN扫描；IP段扫描；TCP反向ldent扫描
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">
      扫描器举例：X-SCAN
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TCP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      会话劫持
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (TCP Hijack)
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      攻击者截获和重定向客户与服务器之间的数据流，使之经过攻击者的机器。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      对于客户和服务器来说，它们都认为是在直接进行通信。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TCP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      会话劫持涉及的具体手段：去同步
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (Desynchronization)
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      常用攻击手段分析：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      信任与认证（常见于
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Unix/Linux)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ；伪造
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      地址及其原理；
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      序列号猜测；利用
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TCP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      定时器漏洞实现的攻击；
     </span>
     <span style="mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt">
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      UDP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      协议
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ARP/RARP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      协议
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      包是被封装在以太网帧内的。以太网有它自己的地址方案，它采用的是
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      48
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      比特的惟一硬件
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (MAC)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      地址。以太网头包含源和目的硬件地址。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      地址解析协议
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ARP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      原理
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ARP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      高速缓存的作用：缓存中毒；
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      常见
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ARP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      攻击原理与防范
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ARP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      应当注意的问题：攻击一般局限于局域网内部
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      DDoS/ DoS
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      拒绝服务攻击原理：
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      目前出现最多，也是最难防范的攻击，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      常见
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      DDos
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      攻击工具
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Trinoo
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TFN
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ：
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       UDP Flood
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      攻击，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Ping Flood,
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Smurf
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      攻击，伪造源
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，特殊
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ICMP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      数据包通讯
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      .
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      其他常见流行攻击工具与攻击手段分析：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
        <font face="Times New Roman">
        </font>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       结论：攻击手段不断变化，隐蔽性更强，应不断学习提高以跟上网络安全技术发展
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US">
      <font face="Times New Roman" size="3">
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       第十周
      </span>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">

       教学要点
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>

       <font face="Times New Roman">

        <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
        </span>
        VPN
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">

      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">

      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">

    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">

      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">

      </span>

       </font>

      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">

    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
