    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      VPN
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的安全考虑
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      实现
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      VPN
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      之前，我们不仅应看到其带来的好处，同时应清楚其存在的潜在安全威胁，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      常见
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      VPN
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      应用环境
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      VPN
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      通常用于三种网络环境。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      远程接入
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      VPN
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      安全策略
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      是网络安全策略的一个子集，相对来说它要更细节化
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (Granular)
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      VPN
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      数据安全性
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      VPN
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      协
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      议
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      VPN
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      是基于隧道
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (Tunneling)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的技术。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      VPN
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      隧道对要传输的数据用
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      协议进行封装，这样可以使数据穿越公网（
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Internet)
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPSec
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的引入：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      补充：在网络的不同层次上的保密及特点。针对网络的分层结构，保密层次也分为：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      应用层、传输层、网络层、数据链路层。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      应用层有
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      PGP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      、
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Kerberos
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      和
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Secure Shell
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      等
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      传输层有
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      TLS
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      SSL
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      等。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      网络层，即
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      层主要有
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPSEC
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      等。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      数据链路层，专有线路连接，是速度快，但实现难度大，如银行的
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      ATM
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      提款机。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPV4
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      数据报与
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPv4
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的缺陷，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPv6
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPSec
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      协议
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPSec
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      是一套开放的，基于标准的安全体系结构提供了大量安全特性
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPSec
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的要点
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      两个通信协议：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      AH , ESP
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      两种操作模式：传输模式，隧道模式
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      一个密钥交换管理协议：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IKE
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      两个数据库：安全策略数据库
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      SPD
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，安全关联数据库
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      SAD
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPSec
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的体系结构
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 21pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPSec
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      数据包信息格式，因特网密钥管理协议
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
      习题
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 1.28gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      当使用隧道方式时，构造了新的外部
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      首部。对于
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPv4
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      和
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IPv6
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，指出外部分组中的每一个外部
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      IP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      首部字段和扩展首部与内部分组的相应字段或扩展首部的关系。即指出哪些外部值是从内部值得来的，哪些值是独立于内部值构造出来的。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <strong>
       第十一周
      </strong>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要点
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1
        <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
        </span>
        SSL
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       的作用和原理
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2
        <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
       配置和使用
       <span lang="EN-US">
        SSL/TLS
       </span>
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.5pt">
      </span>

    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      什么是密码组（
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Cipher Suite)
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      SSL
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      握手协议的步骤
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      安全
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      HTTP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      通信
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      SSL
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      最为普遍的用法是实现浏览器和
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      WWW
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      服务器之间的安全
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Web HTTP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      通信。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      HTTPS
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      可以运行在不同的服务器端口，缺省情况为

      443

      。

      (

     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">

    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      防火墙的概念、原理

     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>

    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0cm; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-para-margin-left: 1.28gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      不可信网络
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       VS
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      可信任网络

     </span>
    </h3>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      防火墙的发展
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      防火墙的实现形式：软件防火墙，硬件防护墙，个人防火墙
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h4 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 31.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: -31.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: -3.0; mso-para-margin-left: .01gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      实例：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      CheckPoint
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      NetScreen
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      、
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      NAI
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      、
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Zone Alarm
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，瑞星个人防火墙
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       ICS ICF ipchains iptables Linux
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      上的的移动防火墙
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      说明其各属于哪类防火墙
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      防火墙技术（层次）
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h4 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      包过滤型防火墙
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      应用网关型防火墙
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      电路级网关防火墙
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h4>

     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">

     </span>

    <h2 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      代理服务器的优缺点，传统代理与透明代理，代理的其他服务如
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      NAT
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      等
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
      习题
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ：
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      1
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      如果说防火墙相关的技术主要有三种，它们是？
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      2
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      如果说防火墙的体系结构主要有三种，它们是？
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      3
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      一台在
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      Internet
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      上的计算机，为什么会出现无法访问内网的
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      WWW
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      服务器？（从防火墙设置考虑）
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      4
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      简单的防火墙过滤规则设置为什么会无法使用
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      FTP
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ？
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      5
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      下面哪种防火墙规则更安全和有效？为什么？
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      1
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ）禁止所有服务，只开启有限服务
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      2
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ）开启所有服务，禁止不安全服务
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt">
      <strong>
       <font face="Times New Roman">
       </font>
      </strong>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       第十四周
      </span>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要点
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">

      </span>

       <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
        <font face="Times New Roman">
        </font>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       安全编程中的缓冲区溢出和格式化字符串
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       教学要求
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">

    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">

        <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">

       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       理解安全编程原理及防范，并在个人编程中避免此类问题
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="BACKGROUND: #d9d9d9; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-shading: white; mso-pattern: gray-15 auto">
       讲授内容
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      解决三个问题：什么是安全编程？为什么要进行安全编程？如何进行安全编程？
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      着重分析两类安全编程问题
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      1
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ）缓冲区溢出
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (Buffer Overflow) 2
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ）格式化字符串
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      (Format String)
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      缓冲区溢出
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 1.0; mso-para-margin-left: 1.28gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      程序例子
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      运行结果
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 1.0; mso-para-margin-left: 1.28gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      缓冲区溢出攻击方式
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 1.0; mso-para-margin-left: 1.28gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      编写正确的代码建议
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 10.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 1.0; mso-para-margin-left: 1.28gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      利用
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      CPU
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      技术防止缓冲区溢出
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      格式化字符串
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
      <span style="mso-spacerun: yes">
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      攻击方式与缓冲区溢出类似，也是通过覆盖缓冲区来达到攻击的目的的，
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 15.75pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 1.5; mso-para-margin-left: 1.28gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      利用格式化函数，如
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      printf()
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的格式化字符串
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
      %n
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      来覆盖缓冲区的。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 15.75pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 1.5; mso-para-margin-left: 1.28gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      导致格式化字符串漏洞的原因
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 15.75pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 1.5; mso-para-margin-left: 1.28gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      利用格式化字符串漏洞可实现的攻击方式
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 15.75pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; mso-char-indent-count: 1.5; mso-para-margin-left: 1.28gd">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      针对格式化字符串漏洞提出一些安全建议。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h3 style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 13.5pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      其他安全编程问题：条件竞争
     </span>
     <span style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      、临时文件、动态内存分配和释放
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style='FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman"; mso-font-kerning: 1.0pt; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt'>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US">
      <font face="Times New Roman" size="3">
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 18pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文隶书; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      实验部分：
      <span lang="EN-US">
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <font size="3">
      <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        实验一
       </span>
       <font face="Times New Roman">
       </font>
      </strong>
      <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        远程控制原理与实践
       </span>
       <span lang="EN-US">
        <font face="Times New Roman">
         (DameWare)
        </font>
       </span>
      </strong>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        实验目的
       </span>
      </strong>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l9 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <font size="3">
         1，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <font size="3">
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       通过
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        DameWare
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       的使用理解远程控制的常用操作和模式
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l9 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <font size="3">
         2，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <font size="3">
       掌握远程控制类木马的防治措施
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        实验内容及步骤
       </span>
      </strong>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo2; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <font size="3">
         1，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <font size="3">
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       下载和安装
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        DameWare NT Utilities
       </font>
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo2; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <font size="3">
         2，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <font size="3">
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       使用
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        DameWare
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       截取远程桌面并控制（要求保存成功控制的截图），注意，请在相临的机器互相控制测试，不要对本机进行测试。
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo2; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <font size="3">
         3，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <font size="3">
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       设置
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        DameWare
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       使得远程主机不出现任何提示，体会网络木马攻击的方式。
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo2; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <font size="3">
         4，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <font size="3">
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       基于
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        VC++
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       的带有远程控制功能的源代码分析（课后，选做内容）
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l11 level1 lfo2; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <font size="3">
         5，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <font size="3">
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       将简单的具有
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        C/S
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       功能的
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        Java
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       程序加入简单远程控制功能，如远程运行命令（课后，选做内容）
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        常见问题及解决
       </span>
      </strong>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1,
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       总是弹出“找不到网络路径”错误提示对话框，无法远程登录进行维护
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <font size="3">
       解决方法：在注册表编辑器中依次展开
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       “
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE/SYSTEM/CurrentControlSet/Services/Lan manServer/Parameter
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ”找到“
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        AutoShareServer
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ”和“
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        AutoShare Wks
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ”这两个键，然后将它们删除，这样就可以重新启用“
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        ADMIN$
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ”默认隐藏共享了，最后重启文件服务器系统。
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        实验问题
       </span>
      </strong>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l8 level1 lfo3; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <font size="3">
         1，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <font size="3">
       在上面实验步骤中需要“截图”的位置把实验结果截图保存。
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l8 level1 lfo3; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <font size="3">
         2，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <font size="3">
       根据你的理解，谈谈远程控制软件和木马有何区别和联系？
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US">
      <font face="Times New Roman" size="3">
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <font size="3">
      <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        实验二
       </span>
       <font face="Times New Roman">
       </font>
      </strong>
      <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        网络数据包的抓取和分析
       </span>
       <span lang="EN-US">
        <font face="Times New Roman">
         (Sniffer)
        </font>
       </span>
      </strong>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        实验目的
       </span>
      </strong>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ：
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo4; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <font size="3">
         1，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <font size="3">
       理解被动攻击与网络数据截取的原理
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo4; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <font size="3">
         2，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <font size="3">
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       熟悉常用抓包工具
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        SnifferPro
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       的使用，为后续课程打基础
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">

       实例分析：使用
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">

       </font>

      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">

      </span>
      <font face="Times New Roman">

      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">

       <font face="Times New Roman">
