       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       密码的截图）
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l6 level1 lfo5; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">

    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">

      <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">

    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo6; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">

    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
       实验三

       </font>
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
       使用
      </span>

        SSL
       </font>
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">

       为

       服务器配置安全通信

    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">

    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l1 level1 lfo7; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">

    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <font size="3">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">

       </span>

    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l10 level1 lfo8; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">

      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        IIS
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ，建立测试网页。

     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l10 level1 lfo8; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">

      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">

      </span>

    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">

      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">

       </font>

      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">

       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       ”
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l10 level1 lfo8; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">

      <span lang="EN-US">

       </font>
      </span>

       测试，分析和比较实验前后，网络上传输的信息的变化。
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <font size="3">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        实验结果（截图）：

       <span lang="EN-US">
       </span>
      </font>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <font size="3">
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       用
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        Https
       </font>
      </span>
      <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       访问原有站点，浏览器右下角出现锁状图标。
      </span>
     </font>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <font size="3">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        实验问题：

       <span lang="EN-US">
       </span>
      </font>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo9; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <font face="Times New Roman">
      <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
       <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
        <font size="3">
         1，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      <span lang="EN-US">
       <font size="3">
        SSL
       </font>
      </span>
     </font>
     <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <font size="3">
       是一种工作在哪个层次上的安全协议？
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo9; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        <font size="3">
         2，
        </font>
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
      <font size="3">
       在本例中数字证书是可以修改的，实际应用中如何保证其身份认证的有效性？
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US">
      <font face="Times New Roman" size="3">
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
       实验四
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
       </font>
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
       网络防火墙
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        (ZoneAlarm)
       </font>
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
       的使用和攻防测试
      </span>
     </strong>
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      </span>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
       </font>
      </span>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <font size="3">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        实验内容：
       </span>
       <span lang="EN-US">
       </span>
      </font>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo10; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1，
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      了解防火墙的分类和常见防火墙
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo10; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2，
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      掌握
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       ZoneAlarm
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      的安装和配置
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo10; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        3，
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      掌握针对几种类型的网络攻击的攻防
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <font size="3">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        实验步骤：
       </span>
       <span lang="EN-US">
       </span>
      </font>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo11; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1，
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      下载并安装
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       ZoneAlarm Pro 6.1
      </font>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo11; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        2，
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      配置
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       ZoneAlarm
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      使得允许特定类型的程序（及其端口）访问外部网络或被外网访问，并了解二者间的差别。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo11; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        3，
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      配置
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       ZoneAlarm
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      使得记录通过防火墙的
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       IP
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      及事件日志，并打开查看。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo11; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        4，
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      利用
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       SynFlood
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      攻击进行测试，在未启用
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       ZoneAlarm
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      防火墙时，测试被攻击主机的结果（无法正常访问网络）；
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo11; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        5，
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      利用
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       SynFlood
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      攻击进行测试，在启用
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       ZoneAlarm
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      防火墙时，测试被攻击主机的结果（
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       ZoneAlarm
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      弹出提示，正确选择后，可以正常访问网络）；
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <font size="3">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        实验结果（截图）：
       </span>
       <span lang="EN-US">
       </span>
      </font>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      被
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       SynFlood.exe
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      攻击时
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       ZoneAlarm
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      弹出的提示画面
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">
      <font size="3">
       <span style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'">
        实验问题：
       </span>
       <span lang="EN-US">
       </span>
      </font>
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 18pt; TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; mso-list: l7 level1 lfo12; tab-stops: list 18.0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <span style="mso-list: Ignore">
       <font face="Times New Roman">
        1，
        <span style='FONT: 7pt "Times New Roman"'>
        </span>
       </font>
      </span>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      可信任网络和不可信任网络有何区别？
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
     </span>
    </p>
    <p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt">
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      <font face="Times New Roman">
       2
      </font>
     </span>
     <span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
      ，防火墙的优点和弱点各是什么？试各列举二点。
     </span>
     <span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 12.0pt">
     </span>
    </p>
